Risk_NN discount_NN rate_NN The_DT risk_NN discount_NN rate_NN ,_, the_DT rate_NN used_VBN to_TO calculate_VB the_DT present_JJ value_NN of_IN the_DT future_JJ projected_VBN cash_NN flows_NNS ,_, is_VBZ based_VBN on_IN the_DT long_JJ term_NN view_NN of_IN the_DT risk_NN free_JJ rate_NN of_IN return_NN ._.
